msg:It may be because the hotel mainly receives large groups, and individual guests feel relatively ordinary when staying in the hotel.
Let me talk about the advantages first: call the housekeeper in advance to contact the extra bed. The hotel attaches great importance to it. The extra bed was completed before we checked in. You can rest immediately after checking in, which is very good.
The doorman was very enthusiastic in leading the way, and gave us a general introduction to the hotel's facilities along the way. If he hadn't reminded us that the duty-free shop closes at 6 o'clock, we might have missed it. Thank you so much ğŸ™
The location of the hotel is also good. On Dongyu Island, facing Yudai Beach, the swimming pool has a pleasant view and a beautiful environment. It's a pity that the hotel is currently under construction, which greatly affects the landscape. When entering and leaving the hotel, you will encounter construction vehicles, construction workers, etc., and it is not suitable for vacation living in the near future. However, when booking, the hotel did not indicate that it had renovation works, and it was not reminded until check-in.
Let me talk about the places worthy of improvement:
Room facilities: It looks a bit old-fashioned, clean or quite clean, but the magic is that there is no pair of disposable slippers in the hotel room, and there is no bag of tea bags. As a five-star hotel, it should not even None of these basic content is. Later, I ran into the cleaning aunt in the corridor and asked if there were children's slippers. The aunt said no, only adults, so we got adult slippers by mistake. However, childrenâ€™s slippers, childrenâ€™s toothbrushes, childrenâ€™s bathrobes and other items related to â€œchildrenâ€ are not available at all, so you need to bring your own. Because we only slept for one night and caught the flight early the next morning, we didn't care about these things. However, after the room was cleaned, the supplies that should be replenished were not replenished in time, which still affected the experience of staying.
As for dinner, because there is a big team meeting reception, the restaurant is all reserved, and only the Korean teppanyaki buffet is left. We listened to the advice of the Chinese restaurant staff and went back to our room to order food. The food delivery service card in the room shows that the service fee is free for 24 hours. However, when the order is placed and paid, it is reminded that a 30% service fee will be charged. It is completely understandable that there is a service fee, but it is written in the room that it is free, and finally the food and beverage depar**ent delivers The meal came and was charged again, which still felt a bit strange. However, the taste of the food delivered is still good, which is worthy of recognition. I hope the hotel can update the "free service fee" delivery card to avoid misunderstanding.
